current broker\n    55→     * epoch. Otherwise, NOT_LEADER_OR_FOLLOWER exception will be thrown. This can fence fetch state update from a\n    56→     * stale request.\n    57→     *\n    58→     * If the FetchRequest reads up to the log end offset of the leader when the current fetch request is received,\n    59→     * set `lastCaughtUpTimeMs` to the time when the current fetch request was received.\n    60→     *\n    61→     * Else if the FetchRequest reads up to the log end offset of the leader when the previous fetch request was received,\n    62→     * set `lastCaughtUpTimeMs` to the time when the previous fetch request was received.\n    63→     *\n    64→     * This is needed to enforce the semantics of ISR, i.e. a replica is in ISR if and only if it lags behind leader's LEO\n    65→     * by at most `replicaLagTimeMaxMs`. These semantics allow a follower to be added to the ISR even if the offset of its\n    66→     * fetch request is always smaller than the leader's LEO, which can happen if small produce requests are received at\n    67→     * high frequency.\n    68→     */\n    69→    public void updateFetchStateOrThrow(\n    70→        LogOffsetMetadata followerFetchOffsetMetadata,\n    71→        long followerStartOffset,\n    72→        long followerFetchTimeMs,\n    73→        long leaderEndOffset,\n    74→        long brokerEpoch\n    75→    ) {\n    76→        replicaState.updateAndGet(currentReplicaState -> {\n    77→            var cachedBrokerEpoch = metadataCache.getAliveBrokerEpoch(brokerId);\n    78→            // Fence the update if it provides a stale broker epoch.\n    79→            if (brokerEpoch != -1 && cachedBrokerEpoch.filter(e -> e > brokerEpoch).isPresent()) {\n    80→                throw new NotLeaderOrFollowerException(\"Received stale fetch state update. broker epoch=\" + brokerEpoch +\n    81→                    \" vs expected=\" + currentReplicaState.brokerEpoch());\n    82→            }\n    83→\n    84→            long followerFetchTimeMs);\n    87→            } else if (followerFetchOffsetMetadata.messageOffset >= currentReplicaState.lastFetchLeaderLogEndOffset()) {\n    88→                lastCaughtUpTime = Math.max(currentReplicaState.lastCaughtUpTimeMs(), currentReplicaState.lastFetchTimeMs());\n    89→            } else {\n    90→                lastCaughtUpTime = currentReplicaState.lastCaughtUpTimeMs();\n    91→            }\n    92→\n    93→            return new ReplicaState(\n    94→                followerStartOffset,\n    95→                followerFetchOffsetMetadata,\n    96→                Math.max(leaderEndOffset, currentReplicaState.lastFetchLeaderLogEndOffset()),\n    97→                followerFetchTimeMs,\n    98→                lastCaughtUpTime,\n    99→                Optional.of(brokerEpoch)\n   100→            );\n   101→        });\n   102→    }\n   103→\n   104→    /**\n   105→     * When the leader is elected or re-elected, the state of the follower is reinitialized\n   106→     * accordingly.\n   107→     */\n   108→    public void resetReplicaState(\n   109→        long currentTimeMs,\n   110→        long leaderEndOffset,\n   111→        boolean isNewLeader,\n   112→        boolean isFollowerInSync\n   113→    ) {\n   114→        replicaState.updateAndGet(currentReplicaState -> {\n   115→            // When the leader is elected or re-elected, the follower's last caught up time\n   116→            // is set to the current time if the follower is in the ISR, else to 0. The latter\n   117→            // is done to ensure that the high watermark is not hold back unnecessarily for\n   118→            // a follower which is not in the ISR anymore.\n   119→            long lastCaughtUpTimeMs = isFollowerInSync ? currentTimeMs : 0L;\n   120→\n   121→            if (isNewLeader) {\n   122→                return new ReplicaState(\n   123→                    UnifiedLog.UNKNOWN_OFFSET,\n   124→                    LogOffsetMetadata.UNKNOWN_OFFSET_METADATA,\n   125→                    UnifiedLog.UNKNOWN_OFFSET,\n   126→                    0L,\n   127→                    lastCaughtUpTimeMs,\n   128→                    Optional.empty()\n   129→                );\n   130→            } else {\n   131→                return new ReplicaState(\n   132→                    currentReplicaState.logStartOffset(),\n   133→                    currentReplicaState.logEndOffsetMetadata(),\n   134→                    leaderEndOffset,\n   135→                    // When the leader is re-elected, the follower's last fetch time is\n   136→                    // set to the current time if the follower is in the ISR, else to 0.\n   137→                    // The latter is done to ensure that the follower is not brought back\n   138→                    // into the ISR before a fetch is received.\n   139→                    isFollowerInSync ? currentTimeMs : 0L,\n   140→                    lastCaughtUpTimeMs,\n   141→                    currentReplicaState.brokerEpoch()\n   142→                );\n   143→            }\n   144→        });\n   145→        LOGGER.trace(\"Reset state of replica to {}\", this);\n   146→    }\n   147→\n   148→    @Override\n   149→    public String toString() {\n   150→        ReplicaState replicaState = this.replicaState.get();\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. Otherwise, NOT_LEADER_OR_FOLLOWER exception will be thrown. This can fence fetch state update from a\n     * stale request.\n     *\n     * If the FetchRequest reads up to the log end offset of the leader when the current fetch request is received,\n     * set `lastCaughtUpTimeMs` to the time when the current fetch request was received.\n     *\n     * Else if the FetchRequest reads up to the log end offset of the leader when the previous fetch request was received,\n     * set `lastCaughtUpTimeMs` to the time when the previous fetch request was received.\n     *\n     * This is needed to enforce the semantics of ISR, i.e. a replica is in ISR if and only if it lags behind leader's LEO\n     * by at most `replicaLagTimeMaxMs`. These semantics allow a follower to be added to the ISR even if the offset of its\n     * fetch request is always smaller than the leader's LEO, which can happen if small produce requests are received at\n     * high frequency.\n     */\n    public void updateFetchStateOrThrow(\n        LogOffsetMetadata followerFetchOffsetMetadata,\n        long followerStartOffset,\n        long followerFetchTimeMs,\n        long leaderEndOffset,\n        long brokerEpoch\n    ) {\n        replicaState.updateAndGet(currentReplicaState -> {\n            var cachedBrokerEpoch = metadataCache.getAliveBrokerEpoch(brokerId);\n            // Fence the update if it provides a stale broker epoch.\n            if (brokerEpoch != -1 && cachedBrokerEpoch.filter(e -> e > brokerEpoch).isPresent()) {\n                throw new NotLeaderOrFollowerException(\"Received stale fetch state update. broker epoch=\" + brokerEpoch +\n                    \" vs expected=\" + currentReplicaState.brokerEpoch());\n            }\n\n            long lastCaughtUpTime;\n            if (followerFetchOffsetMetadata.messageOffset >= leaderEndOffset) {\n                lastCaughtUpTime = Math.max(currentReplicaState.lastCaughtUpTimeMs(), followerFetchTimeMs);\n            } else if (followerFetchOffsetMetadata.messageOffset >= currentReplicaState.lastFetchLeaderLogEndOffset()) {\n                lastCaughtUpTime = Math.max(currentReplicaState.lastCaughtUpTimeMs(), currentReplicaState.lastFetchTimeMs());\n            } else {\n                lastCaughtUpTime = currentReplicaState.lastCaughtUpTimeMs();\n            }\n\n            return new ReplicaState(\n                followerStartOffset,\n                followerFetchOffsetMetadata,\n                Math.max(leaderEndOffset, currentReplicaState.lastFetchLeaderLogEndOffset()),\n                followerFetchTimeMs,\n                lastCaughtUpTime,\n                Optional.of(brokerEpoch)\n            );\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * When the leader is elected or re-elected, the state of the follower is reinitialized\n     * accordingly.\n     */\n    public void resetReplicaState(\n        long currentTimeMs,\n        long leaderEndOffset,\n        boolean isNewLeader,\n        boolean isFollowerInSync\n    ) {\n        replicaState.updateAndGet(currentReplicaState -> {\n            // When the leader is elected or re-elected, the follower's last caught up time\n            // is set to the current time if the follower is in the ISR, else to 0. The latter\n            // is done to ensure that the high watermark is not hold back unnecessarily for\n            // a follower which is not in the ISR anymore.\n            long lastCaughtUpTimeMs = isFollowerInSync ? currentTimeMs : 0L;\n\n            if (isNewLeader) {\n                return new ReplicaState(\n                    UnifiedLog.UNKNOWN_OFFSET,\n                    LogOffsetMetadata.UNKNOWN_OFFSET_METADATA,\n                    UnifiedLog.UNKNOWN_OFFSET,\n                    0L,\n                    lastCaughtUpTimeMs,\n                    Optional.empty()\n                );\n            } else {\n                return new ReplicaState(\n                    currentReplicaState.logStartOffset(),\n                    currentReplicaState.logEndOffsetMetadata(),\n                    leaderEndOffset,\n                    // When the leader is re-elected, the follower's last fetch time is\n                    // set to the current time if the follower is in the ISR, else to 0.\n                    // The latter is done to ensure that the follower is not brought back\n                    // into the ISR before a fetch is received.\n                    isFollowerInSync ? currentTimeMs : 0L,\n                    lastCaughtUpTimeMs,\n                    currentReplicaState.brokerEpoch()\n                );\n            }\n        });\n        LOGGER.trace(\"Reset state of replica to {}\", this);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        ReplicaState replicaState = this.replicaState.get();","numLines":150,"startLine":1,"totalLines":176}}}

The core replication mechanism centers on the ReplicaFetcherThread (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaFetcherThread.scala), which extends AbstractFetcherThread to fetch data from the leader broker. The ReplicaFetcherThread communicates with the leader via the LeaderEndPoint interface (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/LeaderEndPoint.java) and its implementations LocalLeaderEndPoint and RemoteLeaderEndPoint. The LeaderEpochFileCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/epoch/LeaderEpochFileCache.java) manages the leader epoch information to ensure proper offset truncation and recovery. The Partition class (core/src/main/scala/kafka/cluster/Partition.scala) implements the ISR (in-sync replica) management with maybeExpandIsr and maybeShrinkIsr methods, which handle the dynamic adjustment of the in-sync replicas set based on replication progress. The PartitionFetchState (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/PartitionFetchState.java) manages the fetch state for each partition. The ReplicaManager (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaManager.scala) orchestrates the overall replication process, coordinating between the network layer, log storage, and replica state.
